affect people using Bitbucket Cloud and developing Bitbucket Cloud apps.</p>

style="max-width:calc(200px - var(--ds-space-100, 8px))" class="css-15u8od2">Deprecation Notice</span></span><span> </span>Brownout Notice: App password deprecation for Bitbucket Cloud<span role="presentation" class="heading-anchor-wrapper"><button class="sc-htoDjs dZgsYF"><style data-emotion="css 1wits42">.css-1wits42{display:inline-block;-webkit-flex-shrink:0;-ms-flex-negative:0;flex-shrink:0;line-height:1;width:16px;height:16px;}.css-1wits42 stop{stop-color:currentColor;}@media screen and (forced-colors: active){.css-1wits42 >svg{-webkit-filter:grayscale(1);filter:grayscale(1);--icon-primary-color:CanvasText;--icon-secondary-color:Canvas;}}.css-1wits42 >svg{width:16px;height:16px;}</style><span role="img" aria-label="copy" style="--icon-primary-color:#6B778C;--icon-secondary-color:var(--ds-surface, #FFFFFF)" class="css-1wits42"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" role="presentation"><g fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"><path d="M12.856 5.457l-.937.92a1.002 1.002 0 000 1.437 1.047 1.047 0 001.463 0l.984-.966c.967-.95 2.542-1.135 3.602-.288a2.54 2.54 0 01.203 3.81l-2.903 2.852a2.646 2.646 0 01-3.696 0l-1.11-1.09L9 13.57l1.108 1.089c1.822 1.788 4.802 1.788 6.622 0l2.905-2.852a4.558 4.558 0 00-.357-6.82c-1.893-1.517-4.695-1.226-6.422.47"/><path d="M11.144 19.543l.937-.92a1.002 1.002 0 000-1.437 1.047 1.047 0 00-1.462 0l-.985.966c-.967.95-2.542 1.135-3.602.288a2.54 2.54 0 01-.203-3.81l2.903-2.852a2.646 2.646 0 013.696 0l1.11 1.09L15 11.43l-1.108-1.089c-1.822-1.788-4.802-1.788-6.622 0l-2.905 2.852a4.558 4.558 0 00.357 6.82c1.893 1.517 4.695 1.226 6.422-.47"/></g></svg></span></button></span></h4></div><div class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">Bitbucket Cloud is transitioning to API tokens to enhance security. As part of this transition, app passwords will be fully deprecated on <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1785196800000">Jul 28, 2026</span></span>. To help you identify and migrate any remaining usage before the final removal, we are running a series of controlled brownouts starting <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1780963200000">Jun 9, 2026</span></span>.<br/><br/><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What’s changing:</strong></p><p data-renderer-start-pos="300">During each brownout window, API requests authenticated using app passwords will fail with an HTTP 401 while Git-over-HTTPS operations authenticated using app passwords will fail with an HTTP 410.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="498"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What you need to do:</strong><br/>You must migrate to <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/docs/using-api-tokens/" title="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/docs/using-api-tokens/" data-renderer-mark="true">API tokens</a> before <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1785196800000">Jul 28, 2026</span></span>. API tokens offer improved security, expiration controls, and centralized management.<br/><br/>To create and use an API token:</p><ol class="ak-ol" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="681">Select your <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Profile icon</strong>, then select <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/" title="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/" data-renderer-mark="true"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Account settings</strong></a><strong data-renderer-mark="true">.</strong> </p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="741">Select <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/security" title="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/security" data-renderer-mark="true"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Security</strong></a>, then <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/security/api-tokens" title="https://id.atlassian.com/manage-profile/security/api-tokens" data-renderer-mark="true"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Create and manage API tokens</strong></a>, and then select <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Create API token</strong>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="830">Select <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Create API token with scopes</strong>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="870">Name the token, set an expiry date, select <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Bitbucket</strong> as the app.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="938">Assign the necessary scopes and save the token.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="989">Update your integration credentials, CI/CD pipelines, and local Git configurations with the new API token.</p></li></ol><p data-renderer-start-pos="1099">For detailed guidance, see the <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/docs/using-api-tokens/" title="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/docs/using-api-tokens/" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">API token documentation</u></a>.</p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0H24V24H0V0Z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path><rect x="5" y="5" width="14" height="14" rx="1" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"></rect><rect x="8" y="8" width="8" height="2" rx="1" fill="currentColor"></rect><rect x="8" y="11" width="8" height="2" rx="1" fill="currentColor"></rect><rect x="8" y="14" width="5" height="2" rx="1" fill="currentColor"></rect></svg></span><h5 class="sc-cHSUfg bAQlGN">More details</h5></div><button class="sc-cugefK erVvyP"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" role="presentation"><path class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">As recently announced in <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/raising-the-bar-on-marketplace-cloud-app-security-together/98750#p-219238-shortening-vulnerability-fix-timelines-for-marketplace-cloud-apps-9" title="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/raising-the-bar-on-marketplace-cloud-app-security-together/98750#p-219238-shortening-vulnerability-fix-timelines-for-marketplace-cloud-apps-9" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">Raising the bar on Marketplace cloud app security: together</u></a> we are updating the Marketplace Security Bug Fix Policy to shorten vulnerability remediation timelines for Marketplace cloud apps. These changes ensure a higher security standard across our ecosystem.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="288"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What’s changing</strong><br/>The remediation Service Level Objectives (SLOs) for <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace cloud apps</strong> are being shortened. The timelines for <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Data Center apps</strong> remain unchanged.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="454"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Updated Cloud App SLOs (Enforceable September 1, 2026):</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="513">Critical: 10 days</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="534">High: 4 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="551">Medium: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="571">Low: 25 weeks</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="588"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Data Center App SLOs (Unchanged):</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="625">Critical: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="647">High: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="665">Medium: 12 weeks</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="685">Low: 25 weeks</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="702">Additionally, we have published the <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace Security Enforcement Policy</a>, a consolidated source of truth for marketplace security compliance expectations, including vulnerability management, OAuth compliance, partner verification, bug bounty participation, and incident response.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="986"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What you need to do</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1009">Review the new timelines: Ensure your internal processes are updated to meet the new cloud app SLOs by <strong data-renderer-mark="true">September 1, 2026</strong>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1134">Check your tickets: We have corrected an issue where some AMS Data Center tickets incorrectly showed cloud remediation dates. If you believe a ticket still has an incorrect date, please raise an <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/14" title="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/servicedesk/customer/portal/14" data-renderer-mark="true">ECOHELP ticket</a>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1348">Watch the policy page: The <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/marketplace/marketplace-security-enforcement-policy/" data-renderer-mark="true">Marketplace Security Enforcement Policy</a> is a living document, we recommend &quot;watching&quot; the page for future updates.</p></li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="sc-fEUNkw duGuhK">25 May 2026</h2><div class="sc-imABML data-renderer-mark="true">Tile</code> component is a rounded square container for displaying assets like emojis, or objects in a consistent, styled way.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="211">The component supports various sizes (from 16px to 48px), customizable background colors using design tokens, optional borders, and adjustable internal padding for different asset types including third-party logos.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="427">For implementation details and examples, see the <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">SSH access to Bitbucket Cloud repositories via <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code> will be removed after approximately six months. SSH traffic is being separated from HTTPS traffic to enable enhanced security protections on Bitbucket&#x27;s public web and API endpoints.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="246">Customers who use Git over SSH must update their remote URLs to use <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">ssh.bitbucket.org</code> instead of <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code>. HTTPS access to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code> is not affected by this change. </p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0H24V24H0V0Z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path><rect x="5" y="5" 000-1.419.987.987 0 00-1.406 0l-2.298 2.317-2.307-2.327a.99.99 0 00-1.406 0z" fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></button></div><div class="sc-fnwBNb fhIIaI"><div class="sc-iNhVCk fZlvel"><div><div class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What is changing</strong></p><p data-renderer-start-pos="19">Bitbucket Cloud is splitting HTTPS and SSH traffic so that <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code> will serve only HTTPS requests. All SSH-based Git operations (clone, push, pull, fetch) must use the new <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto data-renderer-mark="true">ssh.bitbucket.org</code> hostname.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="226"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Migration steps</strong></p><ol class="ak-ol" data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code>.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="629">If your network restricts outbound SSH connections via firewall rules, ensure <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">ssh.bitbucket.org</code> on port 22 is allowlisted. </p></li></ol><p data-renderer-start-pos="756">More details are captured in this <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" data-renderer-start-pos="812"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Timeline</strong></p><p data-renderer-start-pos="822">Customers will have approximately six months from the announcement date to complete the migration. After the migration period ends, SSH connections to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">bitbucket.org</code> will be refused.</p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><div class="sc-imABML hVXNdY" class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">To maintain system stability as our usage scales, we updated Bitbucket Pipelines to only detect the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">[skip ci]</code> or <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">[ci skip]</code> label within the first 200 characters of a commit message. This means pipelines won’t be skipped if the label appears further in a long message. </p><p data-renderer-start-pos="271">To ensure your builds are intentionally skipped, place the label near the start of your commit message, ideally in the subject line. Manual runs are not affected by this change. </p><p data-renderer-start-pos="451">For details, read <br/><span data-inline-card="true" data-card-url="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/kb/how-to-skip-triggering-an-automatic-pipeline-build-using-skip-ci-label/"><a class="sc-cpmLhU bsMgDr" href="https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/kb/how-to-skip-triggering-an-automatic-pipeline-build-using-skip-ci-label/">https://support.atlassian.com/bitbucket-cloud/kb/how-to-skip-triggering-an-automatic-pipeline-build-using-skip-ci-label/</a></span>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div data-renderer-start-pos="1"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What’s changing</strong><br/>We’ve introduced a new Bitbucket REST API endpoint that allows a Forge app to retrieve the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">clientKey</code> of its linked Connect app installation.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="159">This endpoint supports the migration process from Connect to Forge. By retrieving the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">clientKey</code>, the installed Forge app can identify the equivalent Connect app installation, enabling you to perform data migration or cleanup tasks effectively.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="404"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">What you need to do</strong><br/>To use this endpoint, ensure you have configured the linkage between your Connect and Forge apps.</p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="525">Add the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF data-renderer-mark="true">forgeAppId</code> key to your Connect app descriptor.</p></li></ul><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="585">Use the new endpoint to fetch the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">clientKey</code> during your app&#x27;s migration logic.</p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU data-renderer-start-pos="1"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">As shared in our </strong><span data-inline-card="true" data-card-url="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-3052"><a class="sc-cpmLhU bsMgDr" data-timestamp="1777852800000">May 4, 2026</span></span>. To help teams identify and migrate any remaining usage ahead of the enforcement date, we will run a series of controlled brownouts starting <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1776643200000">Apr 20, 2026</span></span>, for two weeks, after which the functionality will be fully removed on <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1777852800000">May 4, 2026</span></span>.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="335"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">During each brownout window:</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="367">All OAuth authenticated requests directed at <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">www.bitbucket.org</code> will fail with an HTTP <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">401</code> error code</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="471">All OAuth authenticated requests which provide the OAuth access token in the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">access_token</code> query parameters / POST body will fail with an HTTP <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">401</code> error code</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="631">The <strong data-renderer-mark="true">Client credentials</strong> grant flow will not issue <strong data-renderer-mark="true">refresh tokens </strong>in their token response.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="723">OAuth token response payloads will return <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">“scope&quot;</code>  instead of <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">“scopes&quot;</code> (See notes)</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="809"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">Notes:</strong></p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="819">The minting of OAuth2 access tokens should always be made to <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">https://bitbucket.org/site/oauth2/access_token</code>. Bitbucket’s API does not mount these urls under the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">api</code> subdomain.</p></li></ul><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="1000">In the week beginning <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1775952000000">Apr 12, 2026</span></span> the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">You can now nominate <strong data-renderer-mark="true">genuine migration blockers or major customer‑impact risks</strong> via the <strong data-renderer-mark="true">“Request review”</strong> flow on <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/jira/software/c/projects/FRGE/list?jql=project%20%3D%20FRGE%20ORDER%20BY%20created%20DESC" title="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/jira/software/c/projects/FRGE/list?jql=project%20%3D%20FRGE%20ORDER%20BY%20created%20DESC" data-renderer-mark="true">FRGE</a> issues.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="127">This flow will allow us to triage and assess requests to address remaining blockers to Forge migration before  <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://www.atlassian.com/blog/developer/announcing-connect-end-of-support-timeline-and-next-steps" title="https://www.atlassian.com/blog/developer/announcing-connect-end-of-support-timeline-and-next-steps" data-renderer-mark="true">Connect end of support</a> in December 2026. We’ll review requests over 3 monthly cycles, then <strong data-renderer-mark="true">freeze decisions</strong>.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="348">Please <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/jira/software/c/projects/FRGE/list?jql=project%20%3D%20FRGE%20ORDER%20BY%20created%20DESC" title="https://ecosystem.atlassian.net/jira/software/c/projects/FRGE/list?jql=project%20%3D%20FRGE%20ORDER%20BY%20created%20DESC" data-renderer-mark="true">review for existing tickets</a> before creating new FRGE tickets. You may also <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/tell-us-what-you-need-before-connect-eos-submit-your-critical-migration-blockers/99433" title="https://community.developer.atlassian.com/t/tell-us-what-you-need-before-connect-eos-submit-your-critical-migration-blockers/99433" data-renderer-mark="true">review the announcement</a>.</p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">We&#x27;ve introduced three new Forge triggers for Bitbucket deployment events. These triggers allow your Forge app to respond to deployment lifecycle events in Bitbucket Pipelines.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="179">The new triggers are:</p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="204"><style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">avi:bitbucket:pending:deployment</code> — Fires when a deployment is pending</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="277"><style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">avi:bitbucket:started:deployment</code> — Fires when a deployment starts</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="346"><style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu data-renderer-mark="true">avi:bitbucket:completed:deployment</code> — Fires when a deployment completes</p></li></ul><p data-renderer-start-pos="420">To use these triggers, add them to the <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">trigger</code> section of your app&#x27;s <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px data-renderer-mark="true">manifest.yml</code> file. Each trigger provides deployment event data including environment, state, and pipeline details.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="605">For more information, see <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/events-reference/bitbucket/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/events-reference/bitbucket/" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">Bitbucket events</u></a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="sc-fEUNkw duGuhK">1 March 2026</h2><div class="sc-imABML hVXNdY" class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">Following this <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/changelog/#CHANGE-2645" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/changelog/#CHANGE-2645" data-renderer-mark="true">deprecation announcement</a> on <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1771286400000">Feb 17, 2026</span></span>,  the Connect Inspector Service is now decommissoned.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="101">We recommend <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/adopting-forge-from-connect/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/adopting-forge-from-connect/" data-renderer-mark="true">migrating to Atlassian Forge</a> for a more robust <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/events-reference/" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/platform/forge/events-reference/" data-renderer-mark="true">Events model</a>, as Atlassian Connect will reach <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://www.atlassian.com/blog/developer/announcing-connect-end-of-support-timeline-and-next-steps" title="https://www.atlassian.com/blog/developer/announcing-connect-end-of-support-timeline-and-next-steps" data-renderer-mark="true">end of support</a> in December 2026. </p><p data-renderer-start-pos="242">Developers who still need similar functionality can use <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://go.atlassian.com/connect-inspector" title="https://go.atlassian.com/connect-inspector" data-renderer-mark="true">the open‑sourced version of the tool</a>.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="sc-dRaagA diWSJy"><h2 class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1"><strong data-renderer-mark="true">As shared in our </strong><span data-inline-card="true" data-card-url="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-2887"><a class="sc-cpmLhU bsMgDr" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-2887">https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-2887</a></span><strong data-renderer-mark="true">, Bitbucket Cloud will fully deprecate support for OAuth 1.0</strong> and <strong data-renderer-mark="true">implicit grant</strong> flows on <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1772150400000">Feb 27, 2026</span></span>. To help teams identify and migrate any remaining usage ahead of the enforcement date, we will run a series of controlled brownouts starting <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1772236800000">Feb 28, 2026</span></span>, for two weeks, after which the functionality will be fully removed on <span class="date-lozenger-container"><span class="date-node" data-node-type="date" data-timestamp="1773446400000">Mar 14, 2026</span></span>.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="328">During each brownout window:</p><ul class="ak-ul" data-indent-level="1"><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="360">All requests to generate <strong data-renderer-mark="true">OAuth 1.0</strong> or <strong data-renderer-mark="true">implicit grant</strong> access tokens will fail with an HTTP <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">400</code> error code.</p></li><li><p data-renderer-start-pos="469">All requests authenticated with existing <strong data-renderer-mark="true">OAuth 1.0</strong> or <strong data-renderer-mark="true">implicit grant</strong> access tokens will fail with an HTTP <style data-emotion-css="9z42f9">.css-9z42f9{font-size:0.875em;font-family:'SFMono-Medium','SF Mono','Segoe UI Mono','Roboto Mono','Ubuntu Mono',Menlo,Consolas,Courier,monospace;font-weight:normal;background-color:var(--ds--code--bg-color,#F4F5F7);color:#172B4D;border-style:none;border-radius:3px;display:inline;padding:2px 0.5ch;white-space:pre-wrap;overflow-wrap:break-word;overflow:auto;-webkit-box-decoration-break:clone;box-decoration-break:clone;}</style><code class="code css-9z42f9" data-renderer-mark="true">401</code> error code.</p></li></ul></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M0 0H24V24H0V0Z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path><rect x="5" y="5" width="14" height="14" <strong data-renderer-mark="true">implicit grant</strong> flows and existing access tokens will no longer be usable.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="473">To maintain access, migrate to a supported <strong data-renderer-mark="true">OAuth 2.0 flow</strong> by following our <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/oauth-2/" changes require effort, and we&#x27;re here to support you. class="ak-renderer-wrapper sc-eNQAEJ jMQAHh"><div style="display:block;width:100%;position:absolute"></div><div class="sc-bMVAic hAwnoy"><div class="ak-renderer-document"><p data-renderer-start-pos="1">As shared in our <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-2770" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-2770" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">previous announcement</u></a>, Bitbucket Cloud will fully sunset the cross-workspace APIs on April 14, 2026. We had previously communicated an earlier date but have decided to postpone this due to feedback from our partners.</p><p data-renderer-start-pos="236">To see the full list of affected APIs and the corresponding alternative APIs that we suggest transitioning to, please follow the “More details” section of this <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-3022" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-3022" data-renderer-mark="true">prior announcement</a>. Based on feedback, we have also released a <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-repositories/#api-user-workspaces-workspace-permissions-repositories-get" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/rest/api-group-repositories/#api-user-workspaces-workspace-permissions-repositories-get" data-renderer-mark="true">new API</a> that allows you to list repository permissions in a workspace for a user. </p><p data-renderer-start-pos="543">To help teams identify and migrate any remaining usage ahead of the enforcement date, we will run a series of controlled brownouts starting March 23, 2026, for three weeks. During each brownout window, requests using the old cross-workspace APIs will be rejected, and affected endpoints will return a 410 Gone error. If you have made the switch to the new APIs, <a class="sc-likbZx rovKY" href="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-3022" title="https://developer.atlassian.com/cloud/bitbucket/changelog/#CHANGE-3022" data-renderer-mark="true"><u data-renderer-mark="true">announced here</u></a>, then you will not be impacted during the brownouts.</p></div></div></div><div class="sc-cmjSyW iZUHLR"><div class="sc-sdtwF ehFeaO"><div class="sc-iYUSvU nqvYh"><span class="sc-cTjmhe jexMre"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" duGuhK">20 February 2026</h2><div class="sc-imABML hVXNdY" id="CHANGE-3071"><div class="sc-hUfwpO kpKjhn"><h4 class="sc-gzVnrw dVAxBW"><style data-emotion="css
